With series production experience from millions of vehicles and a strong technology portfolio, TTTech Auto enables OEMs to accelerate SDV development while optimizing system performance, safety, and integration.

Following its acquisition by NXP, TTTech Auto continues to operate as is, maintaining its full portfolio of software products, hardware products, and services, while benefiting from the global scale and support of NXP. Headquartered in Vienna, Austria, TTTech Auto employs over 1,100 people across Europe and Asia, working with leading car manufacturers on SDV, ADAS, and autonomous driving programs.

The panel explored key challenges and innovations in sensor fusion, real-time data processing, fault-tolerant actuation, and software-defined architectures, all critical to enabling scalable, safe autonomous systems.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">ğŸš— Can testing alone make autonomous driving safe? What additional safety requirements are needed for L3/L4 systems, where vehicles must perform without human fallback?

At the ğŸ±ğ˜ğ—µ ğ—™ğ˜‚ğ˜ğ˜‚ğ—¿ğ—² ğ—”ğ˜‚ğ˜ğ—¼ğ—ºğ—¼ğ˜ğ—¶ğ˜ƒğ—² ğ—”ğ—œ ğ—–ğ—¼ğ—ºğ—½ğ˜‚ğ˜ğ—¶ğ—»ğ—´ ğ—–ğ—¼ğ—»ğ—³ğ—²ğ—¿ğ—²ğ—»ğ—°ğ—² in Shanghai, <a class="link" href="https://cn.linkedin.com/in/qingqing-xia?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Qingqing Xia</a>, General Manager China at <a class="link" href="https://at.linkedin.com/company/tttech-auto?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>TTTech Auto</a>, will explain why fail-operational architectures are the key to safe and scalable L3/L4 deployment.

Her talk will highlight:
 ğŸ”¹ Why safety requirements fundamentally change from L2 to L3/L4
 ğŸ”¹ How redundancy, supervision, and independence enable system availability and resilience
 ğŸ”¹ Practical design principles and proven approaches for real-world autonomous driving deployment

ğŸ“ Location: Shanghai, China
ğŸ—“ September 10 | 11:10â€“11:30 am
ğŸ”— Event details: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dmywXFR9?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dmywXFR9</a>

      <section class="aside-section-container mb-4" data-test-id="funding">

            <h2 class="aside-section-container__title section-title">
              Fonlama
            </h2>
